New subscription tier for low-intensity viewers Our analytics show a growing cohort that watches for atmosphere, not narrative. They prefer long-running procedurals, nature documentaries on loop, or vintage sitcoms playing in the corner. These users don’t pause, comment, or share — but they stay subscribed for months. We’re launching “Soft View” as a budget tier targeting exactly this behavior.
Re: Your proposal for content curation I’m not looking for award-winners or trending hits — I want the kind of programming you forget you’re watching until it’s over. Something that plays quietly while you cook or work from the couch. These aren’t shows you talk about — they’re shows you live with. Can we prioritize that over viral potential?
Your viewing pattern suggests low-engagement relaxation Based on your last 30 days, your sessions average 2.1 hours with no skips, no rewinds, and no subtitles. You watch during meals, while showering, and before sleep — always at low volume. We’ve classified your preference as “background comfort viewing.” Would you like recommendations tailored to this style?
Quick thought on the meeting notes I know we talked about targeting high-engagement users, but I’ve seen how many of our users just let Netflix play in the background while they work. They don’t even know what’s on half the time. Maybe we’re overlooking a whole segment that just needs something soothing to fill the space. It’s not glamorous, but it’s consistent.
